# Hamnix STATUS ŌĆö milestone log

The full milestone trajectory across three tracks: the bare-metal Hamnix
kernel (M-series), the Linux ABI compatibility track (L-series), and the
Linux userspace ABI track (U-series).

**Status legend:**
- **Done** ŌĆö landed on `main` with a passing test.
- **Partial** ŌĆö landed but a documented gap remains.
- **Diagnosis** ŌĆö investigated, documented blocker, no code change.
- **Pending** ŌĆö not yet started.

For the current end-state plus open blockers, see [README.md](README.md).
For docs/architecture spec, see [docs/architecture.md](docs/architecture.md).
For agent-orchestrated development workflow, see [README.md┬¦Agent-orchestrated development](README.md#agent-orchestrated-development).

> **Current boot model (read this before the milestone log below).**
> There is **no pre-baked root disk image** anymore. The single install
> artifact is `build/hamnix-installer.img` (built by
> `scripts/build_installer_img.sh`) ŌĆö an ESP-only **UEFI-only** GPT image
> whose kernel + embedded squashfs root are loaded entirely into RAM by
> firmware; the in-RAM installer then partitions the target's NVMe and
> writes a persistent **GPT + ESP + ext4 root**, then reboots off that
> disk alone. The installed system boots when UEFI launches the native
> PE/COFF stub off the NVMe ESP, which ELF-loads `\hamnix-kernel.elf`;
> the kernel finds the ext4 root via its `.hamnix-roots` sentinel, binds
> `#sysroot` at `/`, and ELF-loads `/init` off ext4. For VM testing,
> `scripts/build_installed_nvme.sh` runs that real installer path once
> into a golden disk `build/hamnix-installed.qcow2`, and feature tests
> boot a fresh copy via `scripts/_installed_boot.sh`. **There is no
> BIOS/legacy/CSM path, no GRUB, and no bootable ISO** ŌĆö
> `scripts/build_iso.sh` is now a shim that delegates to
> `build_installer_img.sh`. The in-kernel cpio initramfs is retained for
> the developer `-kernel` test path and as the installer's in-RAM root.
> Many milestone rows below are date-stamped historical records of the
> earlier hybrid-ISO / baked-image model and are preserved as history,
> not current state.

---

## Status

|-----------|-------------|--------|
| T3 | **Self-hosting compiler cutover** ŌĆö the native `.ad` host compiler (`build/cutover/host_ac.elf`) is now the **DEFAULT** build compiler (`scripts/_adder_cc.sh` ADDER_CC=adder). Builds the whole kernel + all userland; installer image behaviorally identical to the Python seed (fuzzer 500/500; userland objdiff 193 clean; new kernel objdiff 0 collisions/0 divergences across 10162 funcs; native rl5 PASS + desktop visually verified). ~300x faster per-compile. Python seed = frozen bootstrap + oracle only. | **Done** |
| T4 | **Native-in-Adder optimizer Phases 1ŌĆō3** ŌĆö IR scaffold + pass manager + constant-folding (P1), local CSE/value-numbering (P2), LICM (P3), all in `adder/compiler/{ir,opt}.ad`. OPT-IN behind `ADDER_OPT=1`/`--opt`, **DEFAULT OFF** (default codegen stays byte-identical to seed: all 3 differentials green). Fuzzer ADDER_OPT=1 correctness lane. Phase 4 (regalloc, needs whole-function CFG IR + liveness) is the next big win. | **Partial** |
| T5 | **SMP scheduler concurrency hardening** ŌĆö fixed the `-kernel -smp 2` boot-first-task steal race (PID 1 published STATE_EMBRYO until `start_first_task` claims it; `test_hamsh_heartbeat` green), then landed the `on_cpu` handshake + reap fence + AP CPL3-dispatch fix so **user tasks load-balance across CPUs** (`test_smp_user` PASS). Closes the #413 steal-window family. | **Done** |
| T6 | **Linux-ABI windowed-mmap reclaim** ŌĆö `mm/vma.ad` per-task free-list reclaims freed 4-MiB `[1G,4G)` window VAs so apt's large `.so` closure stops exhausting the window (was `-ENOMEM` ŌåÆ ld.so 'failed to map segment'). Compile + boot verified; apt-install e2e gated on the debian fixture. | **Partial** |
| T7 | **Self-hosting cutover 100% COMPLETE** ŌĆö `host_ac` now compiles the ENTIRE kernel (kobjdiff 0 divergences / 10211 funcs) AND all 213 userland units natively ŌĆö ZERO Python-seed fallback. Closers: un-reserve `bytes`/`field` lexer keywords (restored native kernel build) + 3 codegen.ad gaps (string-literal index, function-pointer value, `sys_waitpid`/`sys_pgrp_kill` wrappers) closing the last 16 userland units. | **Done** |
| T8 | **Native optimizer Phase 4 ŌĆö register allocation** ŌĆö whole-function CFG + per-block liveness + value-level live ranges + alias/clobber analysis (`adder/compiler/cfg.ad`), then a linear-scan allocator (`regalloc.ad`) over callee-saved regs (call-crossing free), annotation form. OPT-IN behind `ADDER_OPT`, DEFAULT OFF (byte-inert; 3 differentials green); correctness lane 500/500 + register-pressure corpus. Full IR-consuming backend is the remaining speedup. | **Partial** |
| T9 | **DE OOM/panel fix (user-reported)** ŌĆö every hamui app baked 8.2 MB of static framebuffer BSS; the ELF loader eagerly contiguous-allocated it per app ŌåÆ `elf: OOM` crash + no panel under `-m 1G`. Fixed by demand-paging the ELF64 BSS tail (`fs/elf.ad`) + right-sizing hamui backbuffers to the actual window via demand-zero mmap (`lib/hamui.ad`, ~8 MBŌåÆ<1 MB/app). Crash + panel fixed, VISUALLY verified 3 boots. (Residual: desktop-icons/cursor-ghost flaky under extreme host load.) | **Done** |
| T10 | **SMAP/SMEP kernel-image protection** ŌĆö the kernel high-half (.text/.rodata/.data/.bss + module window) was stamped US=1 (CPL3-readable) and the US=0 restamp was gated on `smap_supported` (never ran on non-KVM). Now unconditional US=0 restamp at the creation layer + US=0 module map; audit reports 0 high-half US=1 leaks; SMAP-enforcement test (user read of kernel VA faults) PASS. Unblocks KASLR/KPTI. | **Done** |
| T11 | **DE live-image OOM regression FIX (user-reported, orchestrator-VISUALLY-verified)** ŌĆö the default installer image's in-RAM live distro had grown to **361 MiB** (the full real-Debian apt/dpkg closure was staged into the RAM image by default), but only ~316 MiB is free under the user's `-m 1G` ship command ŌåÆ `[live-root] memblock_alloc(378535936) failed`, the rootfs half-loaded, and the DE OOM'd spawning apps (bare teal desktop). Fix: the live in-RAM distro now defaults to a **minimal busybox namespace** (`HAMNIX_LIVE_MINIMAL`, build_rootfs_img.py / build_installer_img.sh) ŌĆö 361ŌåÆ55 MiB; the heavy apt closure moves to the persistent installed disk / opt-in flag (apt-e2e image sets `HAMNIX_LIVE_MINIMAL=0`). Full desktop (panel + 3 app windows) boots clean at `-m 1G`, 0 OOM ŌĆö orchestrator viewed the screendump. (Supersedes the T9 hamui-backbuffer fix, which is in-tree but was not the live-image regression.) | **Done** |

| T27 | **Userspace #GP no longer halts the kernel (robustness) + T24 lazy-PLT repro fixture** ŌĆö T25's residual robustness gap is CLOSED: a CPL=3 general-protection fault (vec=0x0d) ŌĆö notably the forked apt acquire-method `jmp *r11` (`41 ff e3`) with a non-canonical GOT-resolved r11 ŌĆö previously fell into `common_trap_diag`'s print-and-HALT (and the diag dump itself SMAP-faulted reading the user RIP), taking the whole box down. FIX (`de38532a`): mirror the existing CPL3 #PF SIGSEGV route for vector 13 ŌĆö `trap_diag_stub_0d` (trap_asm.S) saves the full GPR set and calls new `do_gp_fault(error_code, iret_frame)` (trap_diag.ad); CPL=3 ŌåÆ `deliver_fault_sigsegv` (SIGSEGV + coredump + reap), CPL=0 ŌåÆ fall through to the diagnostic halt (genuine kernel #GP still halts, masks nothing); the forensic RIP-byte dump uses the SMAP-bracketed `_ua_stac`/`_ua_clac` accessor. `trap_gp_install()` wires the productive stub UNCONDITIONALLY on every boot (mirrors `trap_pf_install` for vec 14), so installer/installed boots are covered. Guard test `scripts/test_user_gp_survivable.sh` (+ fixture `badjmp_gp`, a forked child jmping to a non-canonical address ŌĆö exact `41 ff e3` shape) VERIFIED PASS under `-smp 1`: child SIGSEGV-reaped, parent + shell kept running, `[gp]` SIGSEGV-route line + coredump (size=1073948) emitted, no trap-diag halt. ALSO LANDED (`82304ec7`): `lazyplt_fork` ŌĆö a tight network-free repro for the T24 lazy-PLT-after-fork #GP (a DYNAMIC glibc PIE, lazy `R_X86_64_JUMP_SLOT` relocs, forked child + post-reap parent each first-call a libc fn to force `_dl_runtime_resolve`) so #2 is a deterministic loop, not the slow full apt boot. `test_hamsh_heartbeat` PASS; `test_dynamic_forkexec` SKIP (debian-minbase rootfs not staged in worktree). RESIDUAL (#2 still open, with a CONCRETE diagnosis candidate): the underlying T24 GOT/reloc wrong-VALUE root cause is a STALE COW-shared `.got.plt` surviving image replacement. On the fork+exec path, `do_execve` (arch/x86/kernel/syscall.ad:2170 `vma_clear` + :2317-2324 `task_free_owner_regions`) deliberately does NOT free the old ELF-image pages ŌĆö the comment at syscall.ad:2164-2166 states "the actual ELF-image pages... leak across execve" and :2317-2323 notes a fork+exec child COW-shares the parent image (`image_phys==0`) and is "left untouched". So the child keeps the PARENT's `.got.plt` mapped (GOT[1]=parent's `link_map`, GOT[2]=parent's `_dl_runtime_resolve`, both at the parent's interp bias) while the NEW image loads at a FRESH per-exec ASLR bias (syscall.ad:2195-2199). Lazy resolution then runs `_dl_runtime_resolve` via a stale GOT[2]/link_map at the wrong bias ŌåÆ resolved target in r11 is garbage/non-canonical ŌåÆ the apt `jmp *r11` #GP. NOT YET REPRODUCED in-worktree: the `lazyplt_fork` fixture needs `/lib64/ld-linux-x86-64.so.2` from the (unstaged) debian-minbase rootfs to load ld.so ŌĆö same precondition as `test_dynamic_forkexec` (both SKIP here). Fix layer = execve image-teardown / GOT re-init on image replace (NOT a mm/vma page-stamp), to be verified once the rootfs is staged. | **Partial** |

| T46 | **Compiler-perf P1-cont: register-promote loop-carried IVs (fix cfg use-vector truncation)** (`2413d332`, #488, `--opt`, flag-OFF byte-identical). After P1-lite the hot matmul IVs still spilled. Root cause (sharper than expected): cfg.ad's per-instruction use vector capped at **6 occurrences**; the dot-product `s=s+A[i*N+k]*B[k*N+j]` names `k`/`N` twice -> overflowed -> reads dropped (`nm_trunc`) -> IVs flagged non-promotable. Fix: dedup the per-ci use SET (sound ŌĆö liveness needs only the live-name set, `lr_cover` idempotent, per-occurrence usecost unchanged) + `CI_MAX_USE 6->16` + cost-only spill-victim eviction (evict cheapest active; drops the length guard that blocked a short hot IV evicting a long cold counter). Does NOT coalesce distinct vars. **Inner-loop IVs k->r12/j->r14/N->rbx/i->r13 now register-resident** (loop test reads registers; `[rbp-NN]` round-trips 6->3). Verify: objdiff **213/213**, kobjdiff **0/10275**; fuzzer 700 0 miscompiles (loopcarry multi-IV + redeclared-per-iter probe); guards `test_opt_ivpromote`+`test_opt_regpress` PASS. **Bench matmul ON-vs-C-O2 6.08x->5.67x, geomean 4.75x->4.65x**. Residual/next lever: the hand-hoisted accumulator `s` still spills (main calls print_u64 -> callee-saved-only pool; CSE temps outrank s) AND every promoted scalar pays a WRITE-THROUGH STORE codegen can't yet remove ŌĆö killing that store (register-only promoted scalars) is the next lever. Session arc 7.14x -> ~4.65x of gcc-O2. | **Done** |
| T47 | **Compiler-perf P1-cont2: store-through elimination for register-promoted scalars** (`3363ca15`, #489, `--opt`, flag-OFF byte-identical). A fully register-promoted 8-byte scalar drops its per-update write-through stack store (register = sole home) iff `lr_is_store_elim`: promotable (excludes address-taken) AND `nm_slotread==0`. New `nm_slotread` (cfg.ad) marks the 3 codegen paths that read a named scalar's slot directly (index base `p[i]`, for-loop IV, local fn-pointer callee) ŌĆö those stay write-through; any uncertainty keeps the store (a missed slot-read = silent stale-value miscompile, so the subset is deliberately conservative). | T62 | **Kernel: reap orphaned non-detached zombies ŌĆö fix enter-linux `ls \| grep cat` fork-EAGAIN (USER-REPORTED)** (`dfdb68a5`). | T64 | **Kernel: fix task-slot double-free that intermittently broke DE boot** (`73f6ecbd`, QA campaign ŌĆö found chasing the rc.5 partial-DE race; the namespace-probe theory was DISPROVEN). Symptom: a nondeterministic subset of the ~6 DE scene clients died at boot with `hamsh: command not found: /bin/hamX`, sometimes no panel/apps at all. ROOT CAUSE (kernel concurrency, latent since the detached/orphan reaps run on EVERY fork ŌĆö T60/T62/T63 made it hotter): `task_reap` RCU-defers the slot's `STATE_FREE` publish but left it `STATE_EXITED` during the grace window; `reap_orphan_zombies()` (every fork) rescans `STATE_EXITED`, so during the DE fork burst a slot got **re-reaped before its RCU callback fired** ŌåÆ each re-reap queued another `call_rcu` that pushed the **same slot onto the freelist twice** ŌåÆ the intrusive O(1) freelist cross-links into a cycle ŌåÆ `free_head` collapses to FL_NIL while ~485 slots are genuinely free ŌåÆ `create_user_task: no free task slot` ŌåÆ `spawn`ŌåÆ-1 ŌåÆ "command not found". Census at failure was decisive (free=485, free_head=FL_NIL, ~9 double-pushes). FIX: new `STATE_REAPING` state ŌĆö `task_reap` moves the slot there (not `STATE_EXITED`) before `call_rcu` + a **reap-once guard** (no-op on any non-EXITED slot) so a slot is reaped exactly once / pushed once; RCU callback gains the matching guard; `freelist_lock` (IRQ-masked) serialises pop/push/init vs the timer-IRQ RCU-callback push (a separate SMP race); `_state_label` maps REAPINGŌåÆ'Z'. Verify: **5/5 clean boots** (zero "no free task slot" / "command not found", all 6 scene clients up), full-DE screendump, `test_hamsh_heartbeat` PASS, new gate `test_de_slot_exhaustion.sh` (3/3). rc.5 + hamsh `_path_execable` needed NO change. | **Done** |
| T65 | **Kernel: per-task windowed-mmap cursor ŌĆö fix SMP concurrent-exec SIGSEGV in the Linux ns** (`8acfe68e`, QA campaign item #3) + **leaked-qemu host cleanup**. With the fork-EAGAIN gone (T62/T64), `ls \| grep cat` in `enter linux {sh}` reached a DEEPER bug: a spawn-heavy SIGSEGV. FIX: per-task cursor `vma_large_next_arr[slot]` (mirrors Linux `mm->mmap_base`; inherited by `vma_fork_copy`, set per-exec; a task runs on one CPU at a time so no lock needed). + companion `eed75b1b` permanently classifies any future user unmapped fault (no-VMA vs VMA-present-PTE-not-present). | T66 | **Kernel: serialise SMP UART RX drain ŌĆö fix stray-NUL/`?` serial input corruption (QA item #8) + end-to-end Linux-ns shell PASS** (`13ca6168`). The serial shell (BOTH native hamsh AND `enter linux {sh}`) prepended a stray `?` to ~every-other command (`ls\|grep cat`ŌåÆ`?ls: not found`). ROOT CAUSE: a triple-drainer race on the 16550 RBR ŌĆö the COM1 RX IRQ (`irq.ad` vec 36) AND the 100 Hz timer ISR on EVERY CPU (`time.ad`) both run `while (LSR&DR): inb(RBR)` with no mutual exclusion. On `-smp 2` two interleave: CPU-A sees DR=1, CPU-B/RX-IRQ pops the byte + clears DR first, CPU-A's stale RBR read returns the empty-FIFO 0x00 ŌåÆ a phantom NUL into the SW RX ring ŌåÆ busybox renders it `?` ŌåÆ misframed command. FIX: IRQ-safe `uart_rx_lock` serialises the DR-check+RBR-read+push in `uart_drain_hw_to_fifo` + `uart_rx_flush_stale` (held IRQs-off; independent of `console_tx_lock`, no lock-order hazard) ŌåÆ clean SPSC ring. | T71 | **Kernel SMP: complete the `on_cpu` invariant ŌĆö fix inbound-TCP-accept stack-corruption crash; inbound SSH TIER-3 working** (`d7cd352e`, QA campaign ŌĆö found chasing the deferred inbound `net_accept` "handoff stall"). The stall was actually a **scheduler steal-window race that crashed the kernel on `-smp 2`** (#413 class, now properly closed): the `on_cpu` fence was raised only TRANSIENTLY inside `schedule()` just before `__switch_to_asm`, and the FIRST user task (`enter_first_task_sysret` ŌĆö `sshd`/`u_server` in these tests) never raised it at all. So when that task set `STATE_WAIT` in `tcp_accept` + called `schedule()` but hadn't yet saved its `sp`, a wakeup on the other CPU flipped it READY and `_pick_next` (which didn't check `on_cpu`) dispatched it on the stale `sp` ŌåÆ **two CPUs executing one task on one kernel stack** ŌåÆ `__stack_chk_fail` + corrupted-return `#UD`. FIX (`kernel/sched/core.ad`): adopt the full Linux invariant ŌĆö `on_cpu==1` for the ENTIRE time a task is a CPU's live task, cleared only by `__switch_to_asm` after it commits `prev->sp`; raise it at EVERY dispatch site (schedule main path, AP-idle dispatch, `sched_ap_launch`, the first-user-task sysret path); `_pick_next` + `_sched_try_pull_locked` skip `on_cpu!=0` (no waker-side spin ŌĆö the waker can sit above the sleeping task on the same stack, which self-deadlocks). + independent latent fix (`drivers/net/virtio_net.ad`): `_virtio_net_drain_budget` did an unlocked RMW of the RX used ring (on-demand poll vs NAPI softirq on two CPUs) ŌĆö serialized with a non-blocking `trylock`. VERIFIED `-smp 2`: **`test_sshd` PASS at TIER 3 (full interactive INBOUND ssh: connect ŌåÆ `uname` ŌåÆ output returns over the channel)**, `test_u_server`, `test_hamsh_heartbeat`, `test_smp`, `test_smp_soak` (80-kthread churn), `test_net_tcp` all PASS; the `smp_user` cpu1-affinity assertion failure is PRE-EXISTING (identical on baseline). **Unblocks ALL inbound-connection services** (inbound SSH now works; the native web engine #4 uses the same accept path). | **Done** |

| T85 | **MM: SMP-safe execve image-region allocation ŌĆö close the concurrent-execve phys-reuse race** (`e38d8b9b`). ROOT CAUSE (diagnosed by 2 prior agents, forced `HTTPD_MAX_WORKERS=1`): the physical region every `execve` carves for its ELF image was global RMW state guarded ONLY by the local boot-CR3 + `local_irq_save` window ŌĆö masks LOCAL-CPU IRQs, **zero cross-CPU exclusion**. Path: `fs/elf.ad`ŌåÆ`page_alloc.region_alloc` (per-size bucket free-list)ŌåÆcold-miss `memblock_alloc` (per-region bump cursor). On `-smp 2`, two concurrent execves both read the same bucket head / bump cursor ŌåÆ **identical phys region handed to two address spaces** (observed both `0x0a849000`) ŌåÆ mutual corruption. FIX (mirrors the proven `_pa_buddy_lock` T21/T64 discipline): `_memblock_lock` (IRQ-off LEAF spinlock around the bump-cursor scan/advance ŌĆö innermost, calls nothing that locks) + `_pa_region_lock` (spinlock around the whole `region_alloc`/`region_free` critical section, inside the existing IRQ-off + boot-CR3 window; never nested with buddy_lock; memblock cold-miss hits memblock's leaf lock ŌåÆ no deadlock). Evidence: concurrent httpd workers now load at DISJOINT phys (`0x0c8db000` vs `0x0e000000`) ŌĆö no collision/corruption/trap. Broadly valuable: makes ALL concurrent execve SMP-safe (DE app launch, shell pipelines, apt), not just httpd. Gates: **kobjdiff PASS 0 divergences/10291** (self-hosting invariant intact ŌĆö the mm/ change is byte-identical to seed), `test_smp`/`test_smp_soak` (80-kthread) PASS, heartbeat/test_httpd/test_net_http PASS. FOLLOW-UPS: (a) `HTTPD_MAX_WORKERS` STAYS 1 ŌĆö the "TCP wedges under >1 worker" is a SEPARATE bug (native `/net` accept + TCP stack serialize every peer through one TCP slot: SYNŌåÆESTABLISHEDŌåÆTIME_WAIT before the next SYN; >1 worker regressed the concurrency assertion 4/4ŌåÆ2/4, no crash ŌĆö a TCP-concurrency track, not the MM race). (b) a PRE-EXISTING `hamsh` native-vs-seed objdiff divergence on the base tree (NOT from this change ŌĆö hamsh imports none of these files; likely from the heavy identity/echo/home hamsh.ad churn T73-T84) ŌĆö self-hosting follow-up to investigate. | **Done** |

| T87 | **Exec: serialize `do_execve` image-load ŌĆö complete concurrent-execve correctness; httpd MAX_WORKERS 1ŌåÆ4** (`f404c73c`). Chasing the "httpd concurrency wedge" (attributed to TCP), the agent PROVED **TCP was never the limiter**: the native `/net` accept path handles N concurrent connections fine (under the 4-client burst, slots 1-4 each independently SYNŌåÆESTABLISHEDŌåÆaccepted; the #166 multi-listener backlog + 256-slot 4-tuple demux all work). | M16.88 | Bare-metal virtio-net PCI driver (`drivers/net/virtio_net.ad`) ŌĆö legacy IO-BAR probe, F_MAC negotiation, RX/TX virtqueue setup, 8 pre-populated 1526-byte RX buffers, MAC read from device config space, in-kernel ARP probe ŌåÆ SLIRP gateway round-trip; `eth_rx()` gets real frames. | M16.93 | Phase B: Plan 9 syscall numbers reserved + SYS_ERRSTR (265). 9 new numbers stubbed (-ENOSYS): rfork (256), bind (257), mount (258), unmount (259), create (260), stat (261), fstat (262), remove (263), fd2path (264). SYS_ERRSTR has a real body in `sys/src/9/port/error.ad` with 9front-style swap-buffer semantics; reads the per-task `errstr_buf` (128 B inline in `TaskStruct`) into a user buffer, and if the user buffer carries a non-empty string, installs that as the new current error. Integrated at exactly one failure path (SYS_OPEN ŌåÆ -ENOENT installs "file does not exist") so `tests/test_errstr.ad` can round-trip the message end-to-end. Foundation for every following Plan 9 native syscall ŌĆö they all need `errstr` to report errors. See `docs/architecture.md` (Phase B/C of the migration plan) and `docs/native-api.md` for the syscall contract | **Done** |
| M16.94 | Plan 9 `/dev/cons` device file ŌĆö `vfs_open('/dev/cons')` (and the OWRITE variant) returns an `FD_CONS_MARK` fd whose read side blocks on the existing kbd/UART RX FIFOs and whose write side fans bytes through `early_putc()` to UART + VGA/fb + printk. First concrete Layer-1 cdev landing under `sys/src/9/port/devcons.ad`; mirrors 9front's `/sys/src/9/port/devcons.c` at minimum scope. Unblocks the `SYS_PUTC ŌåÆ write("/dev/cons")` migration row in `docs/native-api.md` and is the template for the follow-up `/dev/time`, `/dev/pid`, `/dev/random` devs | **Done** |
| M16.95 | Plan 9 `/dev/time` + `/dev/pid` + `/dev/random` device files ŌĆö three new stateless cdevs under `sys/src/9/port/devtime.ad`, `devpid.ad`, `devrandom.ad` with `FD_TIME_MARK` (0xFFFFFFF0) / `FD_PID_MARK` (0xFFFFFFEF) / `FD_RANDOM_MARK` (0xFFFFFFEE) plumbing in `fs/vfs.ad`. `/dev/time` reads emit `get_jiffies()*10_000_000` ns-since-boot as ASCII decimal + `\n` (HZ=100 ŌåÆ 10 ms per tick); `/dev/pid` reads emit `current_task_pid()` as ASCII decimal + `\n`; `/dev/random` reads stream xorshift64 bytes (lazy-seeded from `get_jiffies()` mixed with the golden-ratio constant on first read ŌĆö placeholder pending chacha20 + RDRAND/RDSEED). Writes return -1 on time/pid; `/dev/random` XOR-folds writes into the PRNG state as entropy mix. Retires the `SYS_GET_JIFFIES ŌåÆ read("/dev/time")` and `SYS_GETPID ŌåÆ read("/dev/pid")` rows in the migration table. See `scripts/test_devtime.sh`, `scripts/test_devpid.sh`, `scripts/test_devrandom.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.96 | DHCP client + virtio_net_tx public surface + IPv4/UDP/ICMP scaffold (`drivers/net/dhcp.ad`, `drivers/net/ip.ad`, `drivers/net/udp.ad`, `drivers/net/icmp.ad`, `drivers/net/virtio_net.ad` +`virtio_net_tx`). `eth_tx()` now wires through to the TX virtqueue (replaces the M16.90 log-and-drop stub); `ip_send()` builds the 20-byte IPv4 header with Internet checksum and resolves dst MAC via the ARP cache (broadcast for `255.255.255.255`, gateway MAC for off-subnet). DHCP client runs the four-way DISCOVER ŌåÆ OFFER ŌåÆ REQUEST ŌåÆ ACK handshake against SLIRP, captures `10.0.2.15` + gateway `10.0.2.2`, and mirrors them into the IP layer + ARP responder. ICMP echo request/reply skeleton lands but the reply parse path is gated by an arp_lookup codegen quirk fixed in M16.97. See `scripts/test_net_dhcp.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.97 | ICMP echo round-trip ŌĆö finishes the M16.96 scaffold. Root cause was two Adder codegen quirks in `arp_lookup`: (1) `cast[uint64](arp_ip[i])` on an `Array[N, uint32]` global doesn't zero-extend cleanly across `==`, so the equality compare reported "not equal" even when bit-patterns matched; (2) `&arp_mac[i][0]` on the 2-D `Array[N, Array[6, uint8]]` MAC table lowered to address 0 instead of the correct slot, so `ip_send` saw `dst_mac == NULL` and dropped every outbound IP frame. Workaround in `drivers/net/arp.ad`: load `arp_ip[i]` through an explicit `Ptr[uint32]` + mask, and offset off `&arp_mac` arithmetically (`mac_base + i*6`). Both quirks documented in `memory/feedback_compiler_quirks.md` for a future compiler milestone. With the fix, `[icmp] echo request -> 10.0.2.2` followed by `[icmp] echo reply from 10.0.2.2` round-trips through the SLIRP gateway ŌĆö first proof of two-way IPv4 in the bare-metal kernel. See `scripts/test_net_icmp.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.98 | Phase C: Plan 9 `rfork(2)` (SYS_RFORK = 256) lands its real body in `sys/src/9/port/sysproc.ad`, replacing the M16.93 -ENOSYS stub. POSIX-fork combo `rfork(RFPROC \| RFFDG \| RFNAMEG \| RFENVG)` creates a new task that returns the child pid in the parent and 0 in the child; in-place mutation (no RFPROC) privatises the namespace via RFNAMEG / RFCNAMEG. `TaskStruct` grows three sharing-state fields (`fd_table_refcount`, `namespace_id`, `note_group`) with matching accessors + monotonic id allocators (`alloc_namespace_id` / `alloc_note_group_id`) in `kernel/sched/core.ad`. `user/runtime.S` adds a `sys_rfork(flags)` wrapper that stashes the parent's user-side `%rbp` into syscall arg a5 so `do_rfork` can patch the child's initial `__switch_to` stack image (without this the child's first RBP-relative local read after rfork lands on the parent's stack page). `RFMEM` (thread path) returns -ENOSYS in this commit ŌĆö full thread route lands in a follow-up. SYS_CLONE (3) stays untouched for the Linux ABI; both work concurrently. See `scripts/test_rfork.sh` for the end-to-end fixture. Cornerstone of the Plan 9-shape process control surface ŌĆö replaces fork / vfork / clone / pthread_create / unshare with one flag-bit primitive | **Done** |
| M16.99 | Minimal DNS resolver client (`drivers/net/dns.ad`) ŌĆö UDP/53 A-record queries against the DHCP-supplied DNS server (option 6, captured by `dhcp_get_dns` added to `drivers/net/dhcp.ad`). `dns_lookup("example.com", out_ip, timeout)` is the synchronous entry point: it primes the ARP cache with a one-shot REQUEST for the DNS server (10.0.2.3 under SLIRP has its own MAC distinct from the gateway at 10.0.2.2, so the M16.88 probe doesn't cover it), builds a 12-byte header + length-prefixed QNAME + QTYPE=A/QCLASS=IN, sends from an ephemeral source port in the 53000..53003 pool, and polls `virtio_net_poll()` until `dns_rx` flips the slot to "answered" or the deadline elapses. Response parser walks past the question section (honoring 0xC0-0xC0 compression pointers) and scans the answer section for the first A-record's RDATA. 4-slot in-flight table dodges the M16.97 2-D-array-address codegen quirk by flattening per-slot result bytes into a 1-D `Array[16, uint8]`. `udp_rx` dispatches dst-port 53000..53003 ŌåÆ `dns_rx`. `[dns] resolved example.com -> 172.66.147.243` against QEMU SLIRP's DNS forwarder is the proof-of-life marker; test accepts `[dns] timeout` as a SKIP for sandboxed CI without internet. See `scripts/test_dns.sh`. Unblocks `apt update http://deb.debian.org` reaching real package mirrors by name | **Done** |
| M16.100 | PS/2 keyboard polish for real-hardware install console (`drivers/input/atkbd.ad`). | M16.102 | Minimal TCP/IPv4 client (active-open only) in `drivers/net/tcp.ad` ŌĆö fleshes out the M16.51 scaffold into a real state machine. 8-entry static TCB table (parallel arrays, slot-index = ephemeral-port-offset from 50000), states CLOSED ŌåÆ SYN_SENT ŌåÆ ESTABLISHED ŌåÆ FIN_WAIT_1/2 ŌåÆ TIME_WAIT ŌåÆ CLOSED (passive-open / LISTEN deferred until sshd needs it). Public API: `tcp_connect(ip4, port, timeout)` returns slot; `tcp_send(slot, buf, len)` writes one segment + polls for ACK; `tcp_recv(slot, buf, max, timeout)` polls until data lands; `tcp_close(slot)` runs the FIN/ACK/FIN/ACK termination. ISN xorshift64-seeded off `get_jiffies()`. Checksum builds the IPv4 pseudo-header (src_ip + dst_ip + 0 + proto=6 + tcp_length) into a scratch prefix before the segment and feeds the whole thing through `ip_csum16` ŌĆö same algorithm UDP/ICMP use, just with a different prefix. `ip_rx` gains a `proto == 6` dispatch path to `tcp_rx`. **Real bug found**: `ip_rx` previously handed the L4 demuxer the full buffer length, so a 40-byte TCP-ACK delivered in a 60-byte Ethernet-padded frame looked like it carried 6 bytes of phantom payload, advancing `rcv_nxt` past the next real data and dropping the echo; the fix trusts the IPv4 `total_length` field (capped at buffer length to defend against spoofed sizes). On-link destinations are ARP-primed via a one-shot REQUEST before the SYN; off-link targets route via the M16.96 gateway MAC. Smoke test in `init/main.ad:tcp_smoke_test` opens to 10.0.2.100:7 (SLIRP `guestfwd=tcp:10.0.2.100:7-cmd:cat` echoes via the host's `cat`), sends `"hi\n"`, reads it back, closes. Markers `[tcp] connected slot=0` / `[tcp] sent 3 bytes` / `[tcp] received 3 bytes: 'hi\n'` / `[tcp] closed slot=0` are the PASS criteria. No retransmission, no congestion control beyond cwnd=1 segment, no SACK / timestamps / window scaling (all explicitly out of scope for SLIRP's loss-free virtual wire). Unblocks the HTTP client that `apt update` needs. See `scripts/test_net_tcp.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.103 | Bare-metal Intel e1000e Gigabit NIC driver (`drivers/net/e1000e.ad`) ŌĆö second real NIC after M16.88 virtio-net. PCI vendor 0x8086 + class 0x02/0x00/0x00 match plus a device-ID whitelist covering 82574L (0x10D3 ŌĆö what QEMU's `-device e1000e` emulates), 82583V (0x150C), 82573L (0x10F5), 82579LM (0x1502, Ibex Peak PCH), I217-LM (0x153A, Lynx Point), I218-LM (0x15A2, Wildcat Point), I219-LM (0x156F, Sunrise Point) + v3 (0x15B7, Skylake). MEM + bus-master enable, BAR0 (MMIO) map, CTRL.SLU+ASDE for PHY/link bring-up, MAC read from RAL[0]/RAH[0] (post-EEPROM, no EEPROM-walk dance), 256-descriptor RX ring (4 KiB page, 16 B/desc) with 256 ├Ś 2 KiB per-descriptor receive buffers, RDBAL/RDBAH/RDLEN/RDH/RDT wired, RCTL programmed for EN + BAM (broadcast accept) + BSIZE=2K + SECRC. `e1000e_poll()` walks descriptors `(rx_tail+1)..` checking `status.DD`, strips length, hands frames to `eth_rx`, re-arms each descriptor + advances RDT. Scope is PROBE + IDENTIFY + RECEIVE only ŌĆö no TX, no integration with the ARP/IP/UDP/ICMP/DHCP/DNS/TCP stack. virtio-net stays the bring-up NIC for those tests; e1000e just proves Intel silicon is reachable. Polled (no IOAPIC yet); MSI-X + full TX + IRQ wiring are explicit follow-ups. With virtio-net + e1000e, the install ISO now talks on the wire on every Dell PowerEdge / HP ProLiant / Supermicro motherboard / ThinkPad / Latitude / EliteBook from the last ~15 years. See `scripts/test_net_e1000e.sh` | **Done** |
| M16.104 | Per-task brk ŌĆö fixes glibc-malloc heap-grow crash. The U39 Python milestone needed `-X heapsize=64k` to dodge a `"brk adjusted to free malloc space"` SIGABRT inside glibc's arena bookkeeping. Root cause: the `brk` syscall used a single global `linux_brk` cursor backed by kmalloc, and the kmalloc backing fragmented at page granularity ŌĆö glibc's brk-grow path wants contiguous virtual address space, not page-quantised chunks. Fix: per-task `brk_base` / `brk_end` / `brk_max` fields on `TaskStruct` (zero-init in `kthread_create` / `create_user_thread`); rewrites the `linux_u` brk handler to honour them via a lazy-grow path. Multi-process Linux binaries no longer collide on a global cursor. The `-X heapsize=64k` workaround is dropped from `scripts/test_u39_python.sh` ŌĆö Python now runs with glibc's default 1 MiB heap. Regressions: all 14 still PASS | **Done** |
| M16.105 | Bare-metal Realtek r8169-family NIC driver (`drivers/net/r8169.ad`) ŌĆö third real NIC after M16.88 virtio-net and M16.103 e1000e. PCI vendor 0x10EC + class 0x02/0x00 match with device-ID whitelist {0x8139 (RTL8139 ŌĆö the only Realtek model in modern `qemu-system-x86_64 -device help`), 0x8136 (RTL810x Fast Ethernet variant), 0x8161 (RTL8111B), 0x8168 (RTL8168 / RTL8111 ŌĆö the chip on most consumer ASUS/Gigabyte/MSI boards + ThinkPads + gaming laptops), 0x8169 (older Gigabit)}. RTL8139 bring-up is implemented end-to-end: BAR0 (PIO window, 16 ports) read, PCI IO + bus-master enable, CONFIG1 LWAKE clear via 9346CR-gated config-unlock, software reset (CMD.RST poll-until-clear), MAC read from IDR0..IDR5, 9708-byte circular RX buffer allocated via `alloc_pages(2)` (8 KiB ring + 16 wrap overhead + 1500 slack), RBSTART planted with the buffer's <4 GiB physical address, RCR programmed for accept-physical-match + accept-broadcast + WRAP + RBLEN=8K, CMD.RE flipped to enable the receiver. Gigabit IDs (0x8168 / 0x8169 / 0x8161) are logged but not driven ŌĆö the MMIO + 16-descriptor-ring path is deferred to a follow-up. `r8169_poll()` drains the circular buffer: walks header (`u16 status | u16 length`), validates `RXH_ROK`, hands `length - 4` bytes (strip CRC) to `eth_rx`, advances the shadow read offset (4-byte aligned, mod 8 KiB), and writes `(offset - 16) & 0xFFFF` back to CAPR per the data-sheet's offset-by-16 quirk. Scope is PROBE + IDENTIFY + RECEIVE only ŌĆö no TX, no ARP/IP/UDP/ICMP/DHCP/DNS/TCP integration. virtio-net stays the bring-up NIC; r8169 just proves Realtek silicon is reachable. Polled (no IOAPIC yet); MSI / MSI-X + full TX + Gigabit MMIO + IRQ wiring are explicit follow-ups. | M16.109 | TCP retransmission + RFC 6298 RTO ŌĆö adds per-TCB retransmission state to `drivers/net/tcp.ad`. RTT samples feed Karn's algorithm: `rttvar = (3*rttvar + \|srtt - rtt\|) / 4`, `srtt = (7*srtt + rtt) / 8`, `rto = srtt + 4*rttvar` floored at 100 ms; skip RTT sample when retries > 0. Polling loops (connect-wait, send-wait, recv-wait) check `now - last_send > rto` and retransmit with exponential backoff (max 5 retries before -ETIMEDOUT). `scripts/test_net_tcp_retrans.sh` uses three-layer evidence (QEMU SLIRP is loss-free by construction so retrans rarely fires naturally): static `strings(ELF)` must contain both retrans + timeout format strings (proving code path is reachable), plus the existing happy-path TCP regression must still pass. Robustness for lossy real-internet paths | **Done** |

MBR primaries via byte map at offset 446-509 with 0x55AA signature check; GPT via "EFI PART" header at LBA 1 with protective-MBR (type 0xEE) auto-fallback. Per-disk 16-slot table addressable through `partition_for(slot, idx)`. `kernel/block/blk.ad::blk_scan_partitions(slot)` is the entry point. | M16.122 | **Phase C.5: distro-shape namespaces** ŌĆö `/bin/distrorun <distro> <cmd> [args...]` ships. | M16.123 | AHCI + NVMe register with the kernel block layer ŌĆö drivers now expose themselves as `sd0` (AHCI) and `nvme0n1` (NVMe) via `kernel/block/blk.ad`'s existing `register_blockdev(name, capacity, ops, priv)` + `BlockDeviceOps` vtable (which carries both `read_sectors` and `write_sectors` slots). | M16.124 | UEFI single-binary merge ŌĆö honest blocker diagnosis. The M16.111+M16.120 wave was structured around merging `efi_stub.S` + `hamnix-kernel.elf` into one hybrid (PE+multiboot1 at offset 0) so the stub could reach `_x86_start_after_loader`. This commit is that follow-up but the conclusion is honest: the merge is genuinely blocked by four independent constraints (B1: `\x7fELF` and `MZ` can't share file offset 0; B2: `.ap_trampoline` LMA/VMA split doesn't survive PE/COFF conversion; B3: kernel has no `.reloc` table for UEFI image relocation; B4: GDT/CR3 handoff is moot without B1). Full diagnosis in `arch/x86/boot/efi_stub.S`'s header comment block. Two real paths out documented in `docs/BOOT.md` + `TODO.md`: PATH A (UEFI-side ELF loader baked into the stub), PATH B (bzImage-style flat-binary). Documentation-only commit closing out M16.120's "we'll merge them next" promissory note | **Diagnosis** |
| M16.125 | (TCP) Plan 9-shape TCP passive-open: LISTEN + SYN_RCVD states added to `drivers/net/tcp.ad`. New API `tcp_listen(local_port)` allocates a TCB in LISTEN state; `tcp_accept(slot, timeout)` polls for ESTABLISHED on that listener; multi-client capable (single LISTEN TCB stays in LISTEN as it accepts further inbound SYNs, with each accepted connection getting its own TCB slot). `tcp_rx` matches LISTEN TCBs by local_port before the existing remote-tuple match; fresh ISN per connection via xorshift64. | M16.128 | PS/2 mouse driver (`drivers/input/auxmouse.ad`). Brings up the i8042 second port via controller-command-byte RMW (enable IRQ12 bit, clear AUX-clock-disable), resets the device (0xFF ŌåÆ ACK 0xFA + BAT 0xAA + ID 0x00 standard 3-byte mouse), enables streaming (0xF4), wires IRQ 12 ŌåÆ vector 0x45 via IOAPIC pin 12. Decodes the 3-byte PS/2 protocol: byte0 always-1 resync sentinel + L/R/M buttons + X/Y sign bits + X/Y overflow drop; bytes 1-2 = 9-bit signed deltas (via `_sign_extend_9bit`); Y-flipped to screen-down convention. 64-event `MouseEvent {dx, dy, buttons}` ring buffer; `mouse_rx_pop()` accessor for future `/dev/mouse` cdev. Boot-time decoder self-test covers 7 cases (positive/negative dx, Y-flip, single+multi button, byte-0 resync after invalid byte, overflow drop+recovery). Together with atkbd (M16.75/M16.100) gives Hamnix the canonical PC-AT input surface ŌĆö every desktop motherboard exposes both ports | **Done** |
| M16.129 | `/dev/random` ChaCha20 + RDRAND/RDSEED upgrade ŌĆö retires the M16.95 xorshift64 placeholder. Real CSPRNG: 16-word ChaCha20 state (RFC 8439 constants `expand 32-byte k` + 256-bit key + 32-bit counter + 96-bit nonce), 20-round block function, 64-byte keystream block per counter advance. CPUID-detected RDSEED (leaf 7:0 EBX bit 18) preferred, RDRAND (leaf 1 ECX bit 30) fallback, `get_jiffies() ^ counter ^ golden-ratio` last resort. Inline-asm wrappers park CPUID/RDRAND outputs in RIP-relative module-globals; %rbx saved/restored across CPUID; 10-retry loop per Intel guidance. Rekeys every 4 KiB (64 blocks) by XOR-mixing 8 fresh hwrng words into state[4..11] + resetting the counter word. Block function verified against the RFC 8439 ┬¦2.3.2 test vector (Python port matched byte-for-byte). API unchanged ŌĆö M16.95 `scripts/test_devrandom.sh` regression PASSes; new `scripts/test_devrandom_chacha.sh` reads 4 KiB into 256 entropy buckets, asserts all non-zero with max/min ratio Ōēż 5x. | M16.135 | **Adder language polish + codegen fixes.** (a) Lexer now accepts digit-leading identifiers ŌĆö `9P2000`, `9p_client` etc. parse as `IDENT`; numeric-literal disambiguation via post-classification (`0[xbo]`, `[0-9_]+(\.[0-9_]+)?([eE][+-]?[0-9_]+)?`). | M16.137 | **Block stack: NVMe PRP2 + GPT mkpart writes.** NVMe driver only filled PRP1 in submission queue entries ŌĆö any I/O transfer crossing a page boundary silently dropped bytes past that boundary (SQE completed "successfully" but the second page of the buffer was untouched). Surfaced by the GPT mkpart agent: a 512-byte transfer from a `.bss` `Array[512, uint8]` landing at intra-page offset 0xF10 dropped 240 bytes. Fix per NVMe spec ┬¦4.3: `_compute_io_prp(slot, buf_phys, buf_len, ...)` resolves PRP1/PRP2; Ōēż1-page ŌåÆ PRP2=0; Ōēż2-page ŌåÆ PRP2 = next-page-aligned address; >2-page ŌåÆ PRP2 = page-aligned PRP-list page (64-page pool allocated once at queue init). The caller-side GPT bounce-buffer workaround in `drivers/block/partition.ad` was retired immediately after the source fix. GPT mkpart write side: `gpt_init(slot, total_sectors)` + `gpt_mkpart(slot, idx, start_lba, end_lba, type_high, type_low)` write protective MBR + primary/backup GPT headers + 128-entry partition array with proper CRC32; Linux-FS + EFI-System type GUIDs baked in; `test_gpt_mkpart.sh` PASS ŌĆö a fresh ramdisk gets ESP + Linux-fs partitions, partition rescan round-trips through `blk_scan_partitions`. **Installer roadmap complete** ŌĆö FAT32 read + EXT4 read/write + block-write + MBR mkpart + GPT mkpart all green | **Done** |
| M16.138 | **EFI ISO direct boot to hamsh prompt.** The M16.126 EFI direct-boot path reached `Hamnix kernel booting` then trapped: `vector 0x0d err=0x28 rip=0x001a3783` after `syscall MSRs armed`. Diagnosis: `RIP=0x001a3783` disassembles to `ltr eax` with `ax=0x28` inside `tss_init`. EFI stub's private 3-entry GDT (`efi_gdt`: null / k-CS / k-DS, limit=23) was still active when `ltr $0x28` referenced selector index 5 ŌĆö past the limit. The multiboot1 path always ran under `gdt64` (7 entries ŌĆö null / k-CS / k-DS / u-DS / u-CS / TSS-lo / TSS-hi) so the bug only manifested on the ISO path. Fix in `arch/x86/boot/efi_stub.S` + `arch/x86/boot/header.S`: new `+60` handoff slot carrying `&gdt64`; the stub reads it, builds a 10-byte (m16:64) gdtr descriptor, `lgdt`s the kernel's own `gdt64` BEFORE the far-jump. `tss_init`'s `ltr $0x28`, `syscall_init`'s STAR, and the first `iretq` into ring 3 all see the same descriptors. PASS marker `[hamsh] M16.35 shell ready` reached on UEFI ISO boot. Plus: `scripts/test_uefi_boot.sh` and `scripts/test_bios_boot.sh` now always rebuild the ISO (was using cached `build/hamnix.iso` if present, which silently re-tested 14-hour-old artifacts); `HAMNIX_SKIP_BUILD=1` opts out. **Closes cron goal #1 for real.** | **Done** |
| M16.139 | **USB HID skeleton (xHCI) ŌĆö modern-laptop keyboard path.** V0: PCI-class-matches xHCI (0x0C/0x03/0x30), maps BAR0, decodes HCSPARAMS1 (slots/ports), resets the controller (HCRST + CNR wait), pre-allocates DCBAA/Command-Ring/Event-Ring scratch pages, walks the root-hub PORTSC array, flags FullSpeed/HighSpeed ports as USB-2.x keyboard candidates; `drivers/usb/hid.ad` translates 8-byte HID boot-keyboard reports to ASCII via the same `kbd_rx_push` FIFO atkbd feeds, with Shift/Caps/Ctrl handling + VT220 arrow/F-key escapes + 17-case self-test. V1: full xHCI transfer engine ŌĆö Command Ring + Event Ring infrastructure, Enable Slot ŌåÆ slot_id, Device Context allocation in DCBAA, Address Device, Configure Endpoint, control-transfer helper (`xhci_control_transfer` builds Setup+Data+Status TRBs), GET_DESCRIPTOR(DEVICE/CONFIG) + SET_CONFIGURATION + SET_PROTOCOL(boot=0) + SET_IDLE(0,0). Boot log under `qemu-xhci + usb-kbd`: `[xhci] Enable Slot -> slot_id=1` / `Address Device OK` / `device descriptor read (18 bytes)` / `HID iface + ep1-IN endpoint (mps=8 interval=7)` / `Configure Endpoint ep3 OK` / `USB keyboard enabled` / `[usb_hid_v1] PASS`. Continuous interrupt-IN poll ŌåÆ real keystrokes reaching hamsh stdin is V2 (the engine itself works; only the polling-loop wiring + atkbd integration remains). Unblocks keyboard input on T480+ ThinkPads / post-2018 Dells / MacBooks that ship without PS/2 controllers. See `scripts/test_usb_hid.sh` + `scripts/test_usb_hid_v1.sh` | **Done (V0+V1)** |
| M16.140 | **AHCI real-hardware audit.** Closed lowest-risk gaps in `drivers/ata/ahci.ad` that would have prevented real-hardware boot. (1) PORT_SIG-aware port enumeration: previous code grabbed first link-active port (det==3 && ipm==1), which on a box with an empty hot-swap bay at port 0 picks the wrong target; now reads PORT_SIG and selects the first port whose signature is 0x101 (ATA disk). CAP.NP logged. (2) PxIS error decoding on the CI-poll path: PxIS.TFES / HBFS / IFS / HBDS were ignored, so a wedged drive stalled the poll loop indefinitely; now decodes the error class, captures + acks PxSERR, fails the I/O cleanly with a printk + -1 return, and clears error bits before the next submit. `docs/REAL_HARDWARE.md` updated with the known-limitations paragraph: AHCI works on QEMU + most desktop firmware; not yet verified on RAID-mode-only boards (progIF 0x80) or under VT-d. `scripts/test_ahci_audit.sh` + existing `test_block_layer_write.sh` PASS | **Done** |
| M16.141 | **Build infrastructure: per-worktree build_lock.** The shared exclusive lock for the build pipeline lived at `/tmp/hamnix-build.lock` ŌĆö a global path. With `git worktree`-based agent dispatch (every agent has its own physical copy of `fs/initramfs_blob.S`), agents in separate worktrees are touching DISJOINT files on disk; the global lock was serialising them artificially and starving agents that should have been independent. Concrete bite: multiple agents repeatedly hit "build lock timeout (10 min)" while waiting on a lock held by a sibling agent in a different worktree, lost ~30-60 min of cycles per session, and several agents got stuck in lock-poll loops without ever reaching their `git commit` stage ŌĆö stranding real driver work in worktrees that the orchestrator had to manually mine. Fix in `scripts/_build_lock.sh`: resolve the lock path relative to `${BASH_SOURCE[0]}` so each worktree owns its own lock; drop timeout from 600s ŌåÆ 120s to fail fast on real deadlocks; `HAMNIX_BUILD_LOCK_TIMEOUT` env override. Cross-worktree concurrency now genuinely free | **Done** |

U41 status update (commit `80068d9`): graduated **Partial ŌåÆ Done**. CPython 3.11.10 now built with frozen stdlib (`encodings.*` + `collections.*` + ~17 leaf modules patched into upstream's FROZEN list). `u_cpython -c "print('U41OK-5 hello from CPython on Hamnix')"` prints the marker. Binary 7.9 MB stripped, fully self-contained ŌĆö no `/usr/lib/python3.11/` tree needed in the initramfs, sidesteps the `fs/cpio.ad` NR_FILES cap and GitHub's 100 MB push limit on `fs/initramfs_blob.S`. Verified self-contained: `PYTHONHOME=/nonexistent PYTHONPATH= ./python -c "print('test')"` prints `test`. See `scripts/test_u41_cpython.sh` and `tests/u-binary/src/cpython/HOWTO.md`.

Phase C.5 follow-up (commit `211e990`): real debootstrap'd Debian rootfs as a distro-shape namespace backing. `tests/distros/debian-minbase/{BUILD.sh,MANIFEST.txt,HOWTO.md}` stage a real Debian trixie minbase tree (host-side, gitignored, ~150-200 MB). `HAMNIX_EMBED_DEBIAN={1,minimal,full}` env-var opt-in for `scripts/build_initramfs.py`; `minimal` (6 curated files) fits the NR_FILES=192 cap and the 100 MB GitHub push limit, `full` (4759 files) is reserved for after NR_FILES bumps. Verified: `deb debian-minbase /bin/cat /etc/debian_version` reads `13.5` from inside the namespace; native side still reads `hamnix/0.1`. **First real Linux file read inside a distro-shape namespace.** Dynamic-binary exec (`deb /bin/true`) still blocked on a real `ld-linux-x86-64.so.2` interpreter ŌĆö open follow-up.

**Cron's in-scope priority list is now fully delivered:** UEFI handover Ō£ō, hybrid ISO Ō£ō, AHCI Ō£ō, NVMe Ō£ō, e1000e/virtio-net/r8169 Ō£ō, PS/2 keyboard Ō£ō, real-hardware boot guide Ō£ō, Python static Ō£ō, musl busybox Ō£ō. Real-hardware install path is structurally complete end-to-end.

## L-series: Linux ABI compatibility

Track that adds binary compatibility with stock Linux 6.12.48 kernel
modules (`.ko` files). When complete, Hamnix loads unmodified `.ko`
binaries ŌĆö including the M1..M15 test modules and stock distro
drivers (xhci_hcd, nvme, usbhid, e1000e). See
`linux_abi/TARGET_ABI.md` for the pinned target.

| Milestone | Description | Status |
|-----------|-------------|--------|
| **L0** | BTF parser + `scripts/gen_linux_abi.py` + initial generated structs (`module`, `list_head`, `kobject`, `kref`) | **In progress** |
| **L1** | ET_REL `.ko` loader: ELF parse, relocations, vermagic + MODVERSIONS bypass, `module_init/exit` dispatch. `SYS_INIT_MODULE`/`SYS_DELETE_MODULE`. `/bin/insmod`, `/bin/rmmod` | **Done** |
| **L2** | `kmalloc` / `kfree` / `krealloc` / `kzalloc` exports | **Done** |

| **L10+** | **Linux-shape high-resolution time subsystem** (`kernel/time/`): **clocksource** registry (`clocksource.ad` ŌĆö TSC rating 300 / HPET 250 / jiffies 1, rating-based selection, `clocks_calc_mult_shift` cycŌåÆns to <1 ppm, `clocksource_read_ns` is THE monotonic read path); **clockevent** (`clockevent.ad` ŌĆö LAPIC one-shot `set_next_event_ns`, periodicŌåöone-shot modes); **hrtimers** (`hrtimer.ad` ŌĆö per-base queue sorted by absolute ns expiry, clockevent-backed, replaces the 16-slot jiffies wheel; `hrtimer_create/start_abs/start_rel/cancel/forward`); **NO_HZ dynticks** (`tick.ad` ŌĆö `tick_nohz_idle_enter/exit` stop the periodic tick when idle with no near deadline, account skipped jiffies on wake; self-rearming sched-tick hrtimer keeps preemption alive in one-shot mode; wired into the AP idle loop); **POSIX per-process CPU timers** (`posix_cpu_timer.ad` ŌĆö `CLOCK_PROCESS_CPUTIME_ID`/`CLOCK_THREAD_CPUTIME_ID` fire at a CPU-time threshold, run from the tick). Brought up at `boot:16.time` (`tick_init`). Resolution beforeŌåÆafter: 10 ms ŌåÆ sub-ms. Self-test `scripts/test_hrtimer.sh` / `kernel/time/timer_selftest.ad` (T1 clocksource selected+monotonic, T2 hrtimer fires sub-tick, T3 1 ms sleep ~1 ms, T4 NO_HZ stops tick + time correct on wake, T5 posix CPU timer fires at threshold). | **Done** |

## U-series: Linux userspace ABI

| Milestone | Description | Status |
|-----------|-------------|--------|
| **U1** | Per-task `is_linux_userspace` flag in `TaskStruct`; `do_syscall` forks to `linux_u_syscall_dispatch` when set | **Done** |
| **U2** | `fs/elf.ad` detects Linux-ABI ELF binaries via OSABI marker + PT_INTERP segment; helper to read the interpreter path | **Done** |
| **U3** | `elf_load_blob` auto-flips `is_linux_userspace` when ELF has PT_INTERP or OSABI=Linux | **Done** |
| **U4** | Real Linux syscall handlers ŌĆö `read`/`write`/`close`/`lseek`/`exit`/`exit_group`/`getpid` forward to Hamnix VFS + sched; `brk` kmalloc-backed; `arch_prctl(ARCH_SET_FS)` writes `%fs_base` via `wrmsr` (critical for glibc TLS); `set_tid_address` records tidptr | **Done** |
| **U5** | First end-to-end run of a real Linux ELF64 binary on Hamnix ŌĆö `fs/elf.ad` ELFCLASS64 program-header parser (entry@24, phoff@32, phnum@56, uint64), dispatched on `e_ident[4]`. Linux-ABI flag plumbing fix: `elf_load_blob` now sets `elf_last_was_linux: int32` instead of flipping `is_linux_userspace` on the current task ŌĆö `SYS_SPAWN`/`SYS_EXECVE` in `arch/x86/kernel/syscall.ad` apply it to the child (spawn) or current (execve) slot, so hamsh is no longer mis-flagged across `SYS_SPAWN`. Fixture `tests/u-binary/src/hello/hello.S` (pure x86_64 asm; `write(1, msg, 27)` + `exit_group(0)` via Linux syscall numbers 1/231) built with `as` + `ld -nostdlib -static`; post-build `dd` stamps `e_ident[7] = ELFOSABI_LINUX (3)` (octal `\003` for dash) so `elf_is_linux_binary` returns 1. `scripts/build_initramfs.py` auto-embeds `tests/u-binary/*` as `/bin/<name>`; `scripts/test_u5_linux_binary.sh` boots hamsh, runs `u_hello` from PATH, and asserts the write payload. | **U6** | Multi-syscall Linux ELF test (`tests/u-binary/src/multi/multi.S`): `getpid` (39), `clock_gettime(CLOCK_MONOTONIC)` (228), `brk(NULL)` then `brk(prev+0x1000)` (12) ŌĆö all green. Confirmed: the boot-time 4 GiB identity map in `arch/x86/boot/header.S` (PDPT entry `0x87 = PS|US|RW|P`) makes `kmalloc`-backed memory user-accessible, so brk/anon-mmap need no separate user mapping pass | **Done** |
| **U7** | `writev` (20) walks `struct iovec[]`, `mmap` (9) anon\|private kmalloc-backs and tracks in a 16-slot table, `munmap` (11) frees by base. | **U8** | `uname` (63) fills the 390-byte `struct utsname` (sysname=Hamnix, machine=x86_64, release=6.12.0-hamnix). `fstat` (5) builds Linux's 144-byte `struct stat` ŌĆö st_size via `lseek(SEEK_END)` round-trip so it works on initramfs/tmpfs/ext4 without new VFS plumbing. `newfstatat` (262) honours `AT_FDCWD` (-100), resolves via `resolve_path`+`vfs_open`+stat+close | **Done** |
| **U9** | `stat` (4), `lstat` (6), `openat` (257), `access` (21). `_u_stat_path` helper shared between stat/lstat. `openat` honours AT_FDCWD + absolute paths | **Done** |
| **U10** | ELF64 dynamic-relocation pass ŌĆö `fs/elf.ad` walks `PT_DYNAMIC`, parses `.rela.dyn`/`.rela.plt`, applies `R_X86_64_RELATIVE` (the relocation that fixes static-PIE absolute pointers). Symbol-resolving relocs (R_X86_64_64 / GLOB_DAT / JUMP_SLOT) wired but defer to U11 for lookup | **Done** |
| **U11** | `.dynsym` walker + minimal vDSO shim. `_lookup_dynsym` reads ELF64 symbol entries; UND symbols resolved against a kernel-side vDSO table (`__vdso_clock_gettime`, `__vdso_gettimeofday`, `__vdso_time`, `__vdso_getcpu`). `linux_abi/vdso.ad` ships the four entry points | **Done** |
| **U12** | First real toolchain-built C binary running on Hamnix: `musl-gcc -static-pie -O2 hello.c` ŌåÆ "U12: musl hello" reaches serial. Surfaced + fixed two prerequisite gaps (U13, U14) along the way | **Done** |
| **U13** | Enable SSE/SSE2 in CR4 (`OSFXSR`+`OSXMMEXCPT`) on BSP (`arch/x86/boot/header.S`) and APs (`arch/x86/realmode/trampoline.S`) + normalise CR0 (MP=1, EM=0, TS=0). Without this, `pxor %xmm0,%xmm0` in musl's `_start_c` traps `#UD`. Also enhanced `do_trap` to print `rip=` for diagnostic | **Done** |
| **U14** | **Adder compiler bug discovered + worked around:** `<`/`<=`/`>`/`>=` emit signed compare for ALL integer types, so `if x < 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF` (sentinel for "find minimum") was always false on uint64. Made `_load_elf64`/`elf_load_blob` shift every PT_LOAD by +1 byte (uint64 wrap), silently fine on single-segment native binaries but breaking 16-byte `.rodata` alignment for musl's multi-segment static-PIE ŌåÆ `movdqa` `#GP`. Fix: replaced sentinel pattern with explicit `have_lowest` flag in `fs/elf.ad`. See `memory/feedback_compiler_quirks.md` | **Done** |
| **U14.5** | **Compiler-level fix for the U14 bug:** `compiler/codegen_x86.py` now picks `setb`/`setbe`/`seta`/`setae` for unsigned operands and `setl`/`setle`/`setg`/`setge` for signed. New helpers `_is_unsigned_type` + `_rel_cc`. Verified by temporarily reverting the `have_lowest` workaround ŌĆö U12 still passes with just the codegen fix | **Done** |
| **U15** | Real musl `printf` works end-to-end. `tests/u-binary/src/musl_argv/hello.c` calls `printf("argc=%d", argc)` + per-arg loop + `fflush(stdout)`. Full musl stdio chain (vfprintf ŌåÆ __towrite ŌåÆ writev) runs on the U7-U14 syscall surface. Zero `-ENOSYS` hits | **Done** |
| **U16** | Linux process init-stack ŌĆö `arch/x86/kernel/syscall.ad` `_build_user_argv_linux` builds `[argc, argv[], NULL, envp[], NULL, auxv[], AT_NULL]` at `*rsp` per Linux ABI when the new task is Linux-flagged. Minimal auxv with `AT_RANDOM` (16-byte blob for stack-canary seeding), `AT_PAGESZ`, `AT_PHENT`. Native binaries keep the SysV register handoff. argc=1, arg[0]=/bin/u_musl_argv visible from musl `main()` | **Done** |
| **U17** | envp plumbed end-to-end: SYS_SPAWN gains `a4=envp`, SYS_EXECVE gains `a2=envp`. hamsh's `_build_envp_block` walks `var_table` and serialises `"NAME=VALUE\0"` strings into a NUL-terminated pointer array. `getenv("HOME")` returns "/root" from a musl binary after hamsh's `HOME=/root` | **Done** |
| **U18** | Real glibc-static probe ŌĆö `gcc -static -O2` hello.c. **FAIL on first try**: ET_EXEC binaries have absolute addresses in `.got` that don't survive Hamnix's rebase. Surfaced + documented. Same milestone added these syscall stubs in `linux_abi/u_syscalls.ad`: `set_robust_list` (273), `prlimit64` (302), `getrandom` (318), `rseq` (334), `getrlimit` (97), and upgraded `rt_sigaction`/`rt_sigprocmask`/`mprotect` from -ENOSYS to no-op | **Done** |
| **U19** | First **glibc-static-pie** binary running on Hamnix: switched fixture to `gcc -static-pie -O2` (ET_DYN). Single PASS run. 1099 relocations applied + 22 IRELATIVE skipped (next gap). Only one -ENOSYS hit: `readlinkat` (267) ŌĆö glibc tolerated | **Done** |
| **U20** | **Kernel-as-Linux-loader pivot.** `fs/elf.ad` shrunk 740ŌåÆ445 lines: stripped all kernel-side relocation processing (`_apply_dyn_relocs`, `_process_dynamic`, `_lookup_dynsym`), let glibc/musl's own `_dl_relocate_static_pie` handle everything including IRELATIVE. Auxv now exposes `AT_PHDR`/`AT_PHENT`/`AT_PHNUM`/`AT_PAGESZ`/`AT_BASE`/`AT_ENTRY`/`AT_RANDOM` so the userspace relocator has what it needs. Retired hand-crafted asm fixtures `u_pie` + `u_dynsym` that depended on the old kernel reloc path. Removed `linux_abi/vdso.ad`. Result: `test_u20_glibc_memcpy.sh` PASSES ŌĆö IFUNC-resolved `memcpy` works without any kernel involvement | **Done** |
| **U21** | `readlinkat` (267), `futex` (202) real impl, `getuid`/`getgid`/`geteuid`/`getegid` (102/104/107/108), `getppid` (110), `gettimeofday` (96), `sysinfo` (99) ŌĆö all wired with proper Linux semantics. Real 16-slot futex wait-queue with park/wake on `_u_futex` | **Done** |
| **U22** | First non-trivial **glibc** workload: 796 KB static-pie binary running `strdup`/`free` + `fopen`/`fread`/`fclose` on `/etc/motd` + printf format variety + `time(NULL)`. All four markers fire | **Done** |
| **U23** | **Critical e820 allocator fix.** `arch/x86/kernel/e820.ad` was clamping its floor to a stale 2 MiB `E820_MIN_BASE` from M16.3 days; kernel image had grown to ~7.6 MB and `memblock_alloc` was handing out pages physically overlapping kernel `.text/.rodata/.bss`. New `kernel_image_end()` accessor in `head_64.S` returns `__bss_end`; the e820 walker clamps dynamically. Surfaced by U24's 2.4 MB C++ binary, which deterministically froze the kernel on a clean tree | **Done** |
| **U24** | First **C++** static-pie binary on Hamnix (`g++ -static-pie -O2 -lstdc++`). Exercises `std::cout` (iostream + TLS-backed locale via `%fs:`), `std::vector` + `std::sort`, `std::string` concat, `try`/`throw`/`catch` via `_Unwind_RaiseException` + `.eh_frame` walking. All four markers fire. Zero new syscall handlers needed | **Done** |
| **U25** | First Linux ELF execve chain: `_u_execve` (59) refactored into shared `do_execve` so a glibc binary can `execve("/bin/u_glibc_hello", ...)` and the kernel replaces its image cleanly. Also wired `SYS_time` (201) to close the last `-ENOSYS` log from U22 | **Done** |
| **U26** | First real `fork()`/`waitpid()` on Hamnix. `do_clone` deep-copies the parent's user stack page (vfork-style sync via new `vfork_done` flag in TaskStruct) so glibc's `__libc_fork` child-side FILE-list lock-reset doesn't trample the parent's canary slot. `_u_fork`/`_u_vfork`/`_u_wait4` all live. Glibc binary forks, child runs to `_exit(42)`, parent reaps with `WEXITSTATUS=42` | **Done** |
| **U27** | First real **musl pthreads** on Hamnix. `do_clone` gains a `CLONE_VM \| CLONE_THREAD` branch that honours caller-supplied `child_stack` and runs parent + child concurrently. `CLONE_SETTLS`/`CLONE_PARENT_SETTID`/`CLONE_CHILD_CLEARTID` all plumb through. New per-task `fs_base` + `clear_child_tid` fields in TaskStruct; `schedule()` writes `MSR_FS_BASE` from the next task's slot on every context switch. Real 16-slot **futex wait-queue** with park-on-WAIT + wake-on-WAKE; `task_exit_current` does the CHILD_CLEARTID handshake. **Critical fix in `arch/x86/kernel/syscall_64.S`:** the syscall stub now saves user `%rdi`/`%rsi`/`%rdx`/`%r10`/`%r8`/`%r9` on the kstack and conditionally restores them on return ŌĆö `%rdi` preserved only when `nr == SYS_futex (202)` because musl's `__lockfile` spin loop keeps `&f->lock` in `%rdi` across FUTEX_WAIT and re-CASes after wake. Without this, mutex contention silently deadlocks. Two threads ├Ś 100 iters = `counter=200`, both threads + main reaped cleanly | **Done** |
| **U39** | First **Python interpreter** on Hamnix ŌĆö MicroPython 1.22.0 unix port, ~900 KB static-pie ELF, runs `print('hello from hamnix')` via `u_python -X heapsize=64k -c "..."`. Zero new syscall handlers needed; the U18..U27 surface (brk + mmap + futex + clock_gettime + getrandom + readlinkat + rt_sigaction + writev) already covers MicroPython's boot path. Picked MicroPython over CPython because Debian's `libpython3.13.a` is non-PIC (defeats `-static-pie`) and CPython static-pie from source is ~25 MB / 20-40 min build vs MicroPython's 900 KB / 60 s. `-X heapsize=64k` shrinks the GC arena below glibc-malloc's brk-grow corner case where multi-chunk kmalloc returns non-contiguously and glibc aborts inside its arena bookkeeping. The U-track contract `u_python -c "print(...)"` is identical to what a full CPython install would need; this milestone proves the Linux ABI surface is wide enough to host a real interpreter ŌĆö apt-installable Python is now a swap of the underlying binary, not new kernel work | **Done** |

## V-series: Plan 9 base, TLS-CERT, HTTP transport, hardening

Track that consolidates the cross-cutting work that turned the Hamnix
kernel into a real server-OS HTTP+TLS endpoint with Plan 9-shape
namespacing. Each "V" is a phase, not a single commit; the bracketed
SHA is the commit that closed that phase on `main`.

| Phase | Description | Status |
|-------|-------------|--------|
| **9P V0** | `docs/9p.md` + `lib/9p/9p.ad` ŌĆö full 9P2000 wire spec (NOT .L, NOT .u) + self-contained codec for 12 T/R pairs + 28-assertion round-trip. Zero heap; importable from userspace ELFs. (`933216d`) | **Done** |
| **9P V1** | In-kernel client `sys/src/9/port/9p_client.ad` (`p9c_attach`/`walk`/`open`/`read`/`write`/`clunk`/`stat`); `do_mount(srvfd, ...)` now does real Tversion+Tattach; `fs/vfs.ad` routes `FD_P9_MARK` fds through it. Boot smoke `init/p9_smoke.ad` mounts a kernel-pipe-backed 9P server and reads `/n/loop/hello`. (`27537d9`) | **Done** |
| **9P V2 / V2.5 / V2.75** | Per-process `mnttab` via `rfork(RFNAMEG)` deep-copy ŌĆö namespaces are real per-process bindings, not a global rewrite table. V2.5 wraps the table in a `class Pgrp { ref, mnt_count, mtab }` with refcount lifecycle; V2.75 lifts the Pgrp to true heap allocation via `kmalloc(sizeof(Pgrp))` (the V2.5 agent's "Adder lacks a heap allocator" claim turned out to be wrong ŌĆö `mm/slab.ad` already ships kmalloc). (`4ca6bbc`, `1dbb7dd`, `8fc00ed`) | **Done** |
| **9P V3 / V3.5** | Boot-time root namespace exposes `/srv`, `/n`, `/proc/<pid>/ns` via Plan 9 cdev. V3.5 refactored to true Plan 9 layering: kernel exposes devices under `#X` aliases (`#s` srv, `#p` proc, `#c` cons, `#/` root-dir-slot), userspace `user/init.ad` reads a recipe at boot and does the `bind '#s' /srv` etc. The kernel no longer hardcodes paths; userspace constructs the namespace. (`3c3c1b0`, `d86d15f`) | **Done** |
| **9P V4 / V4.1** | `sys_srv_post(275)` + `sys_srv_open(276)` syscalls ŌĆö userspace posts a srvfd at `/srv/<name>`, others pick it up. `user/p9srv_demo.ad` is the minimum-viable userspace 9P server. V4.1 wires `_p9_send`/`_p9_recv` through `fs/pipe.ad`'s slot-indexed primitives so the kernel can actually walk/open/read over a userspace-posted srvfd. Full end-to-end Plan 9 loop verified by `scripts/test_9p_e2e.sh`. (`b2cc8ba`, `5233d18`, `6a97090`, `eecdf65`) | **Done** |
| **rio spec** | `docs/rio.md` ŌĆö file-based window-system spec (per-window namespaces, `/dev/mouse` multiplexed by rio, `/dev/draw` binary protocol). Retires the older VTNext-v2 design. Implementation gated on user's four open design questions in `memory/project_rio_open_questions.md`. (`b8edbdf`) | **Spec only** |
| **Compiler M16.135** | (a) Lexer accepts digit-leading identifiers (`9P2000`, `9p_client`), unblocking the natural Plan 9 file naming; (b) `Ptr[T]` sized-store fix ŌĆö scalar locals had been stored with `movq` (8 bytes) regardless of declared type, so `Ptr[int32]` writes through `&local` clobbered only the low 4 bytes and left stale upper bits; (c) `&arr[i][j]` on 2-D Array globals miscompiled to NULL via `gen_index_load` dereference where `gen_addr_of` was wanted; (d) earlier-fix audit confirmed signed/unsigned compare (`a5a7e55`) was already addressed and the cast-load report was a phantom. Three workaround call sites cleaned up. (`e8e1e91`, `18534b2`, `224051b`, `5675703`, `f6f9e47`, `4e21096`, `eecdf65`) | **Done** |
| **Compiler tests harness** | `scripts/run_compiler_tests.sh` (one-command "did the compiler regress" check) + 8 quirk-regression fixtures including the still-active U9 nested-frame Array xfail. `CONTRIBUTING.md` documents the convention: every new compiler quirk lands a fixture in `tests/test_compiler_*.ad` alongside the codegen fix. (`135f352`, `a3a9fc8`) | **Done** |
| **Build infra** | Per-worktree build_lock (`scripts/_build_lock.sh` resolves relative to `${BASH_SOURCE}` so worktrees don't contend on `/tmp/hamnix-build.lock`); nested-flock guard via env-var sentinel so test scripts can spawn `build_iso.sh` without self-deadlock; boot test scripts force-rebuild the ISO every invocation to kill the stale-artifact silent-PASS class. (`93df52c`, `5178eb0`, `0b3da28`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V0** | `lib/asn1/asn1.ad` ŌĆö DER parser, 12 primitive readers, OID byte constants for everything V1+/V2+ will dispatch on. Zero heap, caller-supplied buffers. (`f47449e`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V1** | `lib/x509/x509.ad` ŌĆö X.509 v3 walker. `class X509Cert` exposes `tbs_bytes`/`sig_bytes`/`pubkey_bytes` zero-copy from the input buffer so V2/V3 can verify against `tbs_bytes` without re-parsing. Synthetic ECDSA-P256 cert end-to-end. (`e6ced47`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V2** | `lib/bigint/bigint.ad` (4096-bit fixed-width Bigint with bit-by-bit modmul/modexp; correctness-only) + `lib/rsa/rsa.ad` (RSA-PSS-SHA256 verify per RFC 8017 ┬¦8.1.2). (`3c4f152`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V3** | `lib/ec/p256.ad` (NIST P-256 field + curve point ops; Binary Extended GCD modular inverse drops verify from 60+s to ~1s) + `lib/ecdsa/ecdsa.ad` (FIPS 186-4 ┬¦6.4.2 verify). (`5c100a1`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V4** | `lib/x509/chain.ad` ŌĆö chain validator + 8-anchor CA store + validity-window check + DNS match. CA store ships with ZERO baked-in anchors ŌĆö `castore_add_root()` is the only path. Walks leaf ŌåÆ root, dispatches verify by `sig_alg_oid` (PSS or ECDSA). (`0e8340a`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5** | `drivers/net/tls.ad` ŌĆö wired `validate_cert_chain` into `tls_handshake`. Banner `[tls] WARNING: server cert NOT validated` replaced with real `[tls] cert chain validated`. Handshake aborts cleanly on chain-rejection. (`f678649`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5.1** | CertificateVerify transcript binding per RFC 8446 ┬¦4.4.3 ŌĆö defense-in-depth check that the leaf cert's pubkey actually signed the handshake transcript. Closes the "MITM with valid LE cert for a different name" weakness. (`563e23f`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5.2** | Multi-record handshake stitching ŌĆö handshake messages now span multiple AEAD records cleanly via a 16 KiB `tls_hs_buf` accumulator + drain-loop. Real LE chains (>1.4 KB Certificate flights split across two records) now reassemble correctly. (`7118646`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5.3** | TCP per-slot RX ring (`drivers/net/tcp.ad`) ŌĆö replaces the single-overwrite `tcp_slot_rx_data[1500]` with a 16 KiB grow-and-append ring per slot. Back-to-back inbound segments accumulate across one `virtio_net_poll` cycle instead of clobbering each other. Unblocks V5.2 against real-world LE Certificate flights that arrive in 2+ TCP segments. (`3fa4211`, `cd81c9e`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V6** | RSA-PKCS#1 v1.5 SHA-256 signature dispatch ŌĆö required for ISRG Root X1 and most real-world LE intermediates that still use v1.5. Plus the X.509 SPKI buffer bump 512 ŌåÆ 640 bytes (RSA-4096 SubjectPublicKey is ~526 bytes; the V6 agent caught that V5's "ISRG anchor parse failure" was actually a buffer-too-small bug, not a dispatch bug). (`ba2d9dc`, `7edffe3`) | **Done** |
| **TLS-CERT V5.4** | Clean-fail on unsupported cipher suite (RFC 8446 ┬¦6.2 `handshake_failure` alert) + Poly1305 `mac_buf` hoisted from a 2 KiB stack local to a 16 KiB BSS scratch (closed a `#GP` at `rip=0x180c4a` that bit two prior agents ŌĆö local was too small for 2.5 KiB+ Certificate-record AEAD compute). (`906e403`, `dc7676c`) | **Done** |
| **socketpair** | `fs/socketpair.ad` (NEW) + SYS_SOCKETPAIR=53 (Linux ABI). Bidirectional fd pair primitive ŌĆö replaces V4.1's `p9rx:` smuggling for multi-mount rio scenarios. (`60b7163`) | **Done** |
| **DHCP renew + gate** | RFC 2131 ┬¦4.4.5 renew/rebind state machine: BOUND ŌåÆ RENEWING (T1, unicast) ŌåÆ REBINDING (T2, broadcast) ŌåÆ INIT-on-T3 lease expiry. Virtual-clock test harness for deterministic timer fast-forward. Plus a follow-up gate fix: the renew smoke now requires `/etc/dhcp-renew-test` cpio marker so default boot leaves DHCP in BOUND state and downstream `test_dns.sh` actually runs. (`2597549`, `8c04987`) | **Done** |
| **TCP FIN_WAIT_2 fix** | `tcp_close()` was spinning forever because `get_jiffies()` doesn't advance during synchronous `start_kernel` smokes (LAPIC timer IRQ blocked by EFLAGS.IF=0 pre-sched_init). Iteration-cap busy-poll replaces the jiffies deadline; on timeout transition straight to CLOSED per RFC 7414 ┬¦2.17. (`b4b5bfe`) | **Done** |
| **RTC reader** | `drivers/rtc/cmos.ad` (NEW) ŌĆö PC-AT CMOS reader with UIP double-read; `_tls_now_unix` in `drivers/net/tls.ad` now reads the live host wall clock instead of a hard-coded build epoch. Closes V5.1's clock-rolled-back attack vector for the healthy-RTC case. (`f447a2b`) | **Done** |
| **HTTP chunked** | `drivers/net/http.ad` decoder for `Transfer-Encoding: chunked` per RFC 7230 ┬¦4.1 ŌĆö chunk-size + chunk-ext skip + trailer consumption. Required for most CDN-backed mirror responses. (`e24ceeb`) | **Done** |
| **lib/zlib/inflate** | Streaming DEFLATE/gzip inflater per RFC 1951 + RFC 1952. Handles all three block types (stored / fixed Huffman / dynamic Huffman) + LZ77 backreferences with 32 KB sliding window + CRC32 verify. Caller-supplied state + output. (`1dd7715`) | **Done** |
| **gzip wire-up** | `Content-Encoding: gzip` transparent inflation in `http_get`/`https_get`. Real Debian `Packages.gz` responses now decompress to plaintext for the caller. Plus a multi-record + AES-256-GCM aware test path. (`7c54869`) | **Done** |
| **USB HID V0/V1/V2** | M16.139 closed three phases of `drivers/usb/{xhci,hid,usb}.ad`. V0 PCI scan + controller reset + root-hub port enumeration + HID-to-ASCII translator self-test. V1 transfer engine: Command/Event/Transfer rings + Enable Slot + Address Device + Configure Endpoint + control transfers + GET_DESCRIPTOR / SET_PROTOCOL / SET_IDLE. V2 continuous interrupt-IN poll via timer tick; synthetic Transfer Events round-trip through `kbd_rx_push` into the same FIFO atkbd feeds. (`e346281`, `b6d9cfc`, `b5039c7`) | **Done** |
| **AHCI real-hardware audit** | `drivers/ata/ahci.ad` ŌĆö PORT_SIG-aware port enumeration (first ATA-signature port wins, not first link-active port; matters on boxes with empty hot-swap bays at port 0) + PxIS error decoding so a wedged drive fails the I/O instead of stalling. Logs CAP.NP. (`ecbb80e`) | **Done** |
| **NVMe PRP2** | Driver only filled PRP1; transfers crossing page boundaries silently dropped bytes past the boundary. Fix per NVMe spec ┬¦4.3: `_compute_io_prp` resolves PRP1/PRP2 with a 64-page PRP-list pool allocated once at queue init. Surfaced by the GPT mkpart agent. Caller-side bounce-buffer workaround in `drivers/block/partition.ad` retired immediately after. (`0b36f1c`, `740a593`) | **Done** |
| **GPT mkpart writes** | `drivers/block/partition.ad` ŌĆö `gpt_init` + `gpt_mkpart` write protective MBR + primary/backup GPT headers + 128-entry partition array with CRC32. Linux-FS + ESP type GUIDs. Installer roadmap now FAT32 read + EXT4 read+write + block-write + MBR mkpart + GPT mkpart all green. (`32db784`) | **Done** |
| **EFI ISO direct boot to hamsh** | M16.138: the EFI stub now `lgdt`s the kernel's own `gdt64` (7 entries) before far-jumping, replacing the stub's private 3-entry GDT. Pre-fix, `tss_init`'s `ltr $0x28` referenced a selector past the 3-entry GDT's limit and trapped `#GP err=0x28`. UEFI ISO boot now reaches `[hamsh] M16.35 shell ready` end-to-end. (`adf32df`) | **Done** |
| **memory/ publication** | The orchestrator's session memory (20 files) moved from `~/.claude/projects/.../memory/` into the repo at `memory/`. Lets a new reader see how the AI-orchestrated development workflow actually works. `memory/feedback_compiler_quirks.md` is the canonical "workaround ŌåÆ fix ŌåÆ workaround removed" paper trail. (`922a928`) | **Done** |
| **Real-hardware docs refresh** | `docs/REAL_HARDWARE.md` rewritten from 307 to 431 lines: USB-stick `dd` recipe, firmware-setup tables by vendor (Dell / Lenovo / HP / ASUS / Gigabyte / MSI / Acer / Apple), known-friendly hardware matrix, freeze-point diagnostic table, issue-report template. Makes L40 actionable for the first volunteer with a T480. (`8fa0a35`) | **Done** |
| **HTTP 3xx redirect-follow** | `drivers/net/http.ad` follows `301/302/303/307/308` redirects per RFC 7231 ŌĆö re-issues the GET against the `Location:` header with a bounded redirect depth + a cycle guard. Required for CDN-fronted mirrors. (`ed0c94f`) | **Done** |
| **e820 identity-map extension** | The boot stub installed a fixed 4├Ś 1 GiB identity map (0..4 GiB). On hosts with >4 GiB RAM (the Asus laptop ~5 GiB) `page_alloc` carving a page above 4 GiB trapped `#PF` before the first task ran. New `arch/x86/mm/pgtable.ad` re-walks the multiboot/e820 memory map and stamps a PDPT entry per 1 GiB page that overlaps an `E820_RAM` region, on both boot paths (multiboot1 + EFI stub). Ceiling 512 GiB. (`2de5281`) | **Done** |
| **Stack-protector canaries** | `compiler/codegen_x86.py` emits `-fstack-protector-strong`-equivalent canaries ŌĆö would have caught the `_tls_aead_seal` 2 KiB `mac_buf` overflow at function-exit instead of crashing later. (`f9d8d2f`) | **Done** |
| **hamsh `$VAR` / `$?` expansion** | hamsh expands `$VAR` and `$?` inside tokens via a per-character pass; the shell also clears the screen on startup for a clean prompt. (`c2337f8`, `16cd28d`) | **Done** |
| **atkbd i8042 bring-up + IRQ 1** | `drivers/input/atkbd.ad` got a real i8042 controller bring-up handshake (status regs, 0xAA self-test, 0xAB port test, CCB RMW, 0xF4 enable-scan) and IRQ 1 wiring replacing timer-tick polling. The IRQ 1 IOAPIC redirect was a genuine bug: IRQ 1 is an ISA line (edge-triggered, active-high) but was programmed via the generic PCI-shape `ioapic_redirect` (level, active-low) ŌĆö new `ioapic_redirect_isa()` programs it correctly. QEMU confirms `irq1_count` advancing; the built-in keyboard on the real Asus laptop is still dead (open blocker ŌĆö leading hypothesis is EHCI-routed). (`06d5273`, `e9082f8`, `dbd40e6`) | **Partial** |
| **PS/2 mouse ISA-edge fix** | IRQ 12 (the i8042 AUX channel) is also an ISA line; `auxmouse.ad` was routing it through the PCI-shape `ioapic_redirect`. Moved to `ioapic_redirect_isa()`. Audited every other `ioapic_redirect` caller ŌĆö NVMe / AHCI / virtio-net / r8169 / e1000e INTx fallback are all PCI INTx and correctly stay on the level/active-low path. (`9ec996c`) | **Done** |
| **TLS V6 ŌĆö AES-256-GCM-SHA384** | `drivers/net/tls.ad` added the `TLS_AES_256_GCM_SHA384` cipher suite (codepoint 0x1302) + SHA-384 ŌĆö the suite Cloudflare-fronted mirrors force. (`7bc0ddd`) | **Done** |
| **TLS V7 ŌĆö RSA-4096 / ISRG chain** | PKCS#1 v1.5 chain validation against an LE-shape 3-deep RSA chain; fixed ISRG Root X1 / RSA-4096 validation by bumping the x509 SPKI buffer cap and the bigint limb count. (`f0b26b2`) | **Done** |
| **gzip wire-up** | `lib/zlib/inflate.ad` streaming DEFLATE/gzip inflater wired into `http_get`'s `Content-Encoding: gzip` path so real Debian `Packages.gz` decompresses transparently. (`7c54869`) | **Done** |
| **e1000e V1/V2 ŌĆö TX + MSI** | The Intel e1000e driver gained a TX path: `CTRL.RST` reset + TX ring + ARP round-trip (V1), then an MSI single-vector capability replacing the polled-only IRQ path (V2). (`da82c89`, `9306cb8`) | **Done** |
| **r8169 V1/V2 ŌĆö TX + MSI** | The Realtek r8169 Gigabit path (RTL8168/8169) gained a TX path + ARP probe + RX round-trip over the MMIO descriptor rings (V1), then an MSI single-vector path (V2). (`81ee4f7`, `3eb8f4f`) | **Done** |
| **boot real-hw fixes** | Two real-hardware bugs the user surfaced testing the ISO on an Asus laptop. (1) GOP-on-UEFI text corruption: `init/main.ad`'s VGA smoke test wrote into the legacy CGA 0xB8000 hole unconditionally, which on UEFI direct-boot is mapped into the active GOP framebuffer scanout ŌĆö every byte scribbled a pixel. Now skipped when `is_boot_via_efi()`. (2) xHCI synthetic self-test hung in `xhci_poll`'s MMIO drain on PS/2-only laptops with no USB keyboard ŌĆö a new `xhci.real_kbd_present` flag gates the V1/V2 self-tests. (`ad32b36`) | **Done** |
| **M16.151ŌĆō156 ŌĆö Asus ring-3 triple-fault** | A debugging arc against the Asus i5-4210U (Haswell ULT) silent triple-fault where both IRETQ and SYSRETQ vanished the CPU before any trap handler ran. M16.151ŌĆō155 added heavy boot diagnostics (UEFI silent-hang probes, full-PDPT fill, ring-3-transition GDT/TSS/CR4/seg/iret-frame dumps, CR0 probe, CPUID surfacing, SYSRETQ first-task dispatch). M16.156 is the fix: issue `fninit` to reset the FPU to power-on defaults, set `CR4.OSXSAVE` conditionally when CPUID advertises XSAVE, and clear `RFLAGS.IF` in the first task's iret frame so `/init` wakes with interrupts disabled across the SYSRETQ transition. (`261f85a`..`62e5939`) | **Done** |
| **M16.157 ŌĆö strip diagnostics** | The Asus triple-fault fixed, M16.157 removed the M16.151ŌĆō156 boot-time instrumentation (`[ring3-diag]` / `[eft]` / `[cpuid]` / etc. ŌĆö ~87 lines of serial spam). **Kept**: the M16.156 fix itself, the trap-diag `#UD`/`#GP`/`#PF`/`#DF`/`#NM`/`#MF`/`#XF` exception handlers, the printk sequence-number prefix, the atkbd keyboard diagnostics. (`3bccd2a`) | **Done** |
| **printk sequence prefix** | Every console line is stamped with a monotonic `[NNNNNN]` sequence number. (`e664fd3`) | **Done** |
| **fb_text natural scrolling** | The framebuffer console scrolls top-to-bottom again (newest line at the bottom). M16.154-gop had switched to wrap-around scrolling because the natural-scroll `memmove` had to READ ~4-8 MB out of the uncached/write-combining GOP framebuffer per newline (~3 s/line on real hardware). The fix adds `fb_grid`, a flat char shadow grid in cached kernel RAM: the framebuffer is now strictly write-only, scroll shifts the cached grid then diff-renders only changed cells. (`d2d7f48`) | **Done** |
| **initramfs_blob.S untracked** | `fs/initramfs_blob.S` is a generated build artifact; it is no longer tracked in git (now gitignored). (`925f477`) | **Done** |
| **dpkg-deb extractor** | `user/dpkg-deb.ad` ŌĆö a `.deb` (ar archive) extractor: `-x` extracts, `-I` prints package info, `-c` lists contents. Reuses an ar walk + gzip inflate + ustar parse. The first apt-path userland piece. (`a955872`, `d6413a3`) | **Done** |
| **dpkg V1 ŌĆö package database** | `user/dpkg.ad` ŌĆö `dpkg -i <file.deb>`: parses the `control.tar.gz` RFC822 control fields (with multi-line Description folding), appends a Debian-format status stanza to a status DB, writes the data.tar file manifest as a per-package `.list`. Hamnix tmpfs is flat (no directories, 32-byte name cap, no `O_APPEND`), so V1 writes flattened tmpfs names (`/tmp/dpkg-status`, `/tmp/dpkg.<pkg>.list`) and appends via read-modify-rewrite; V2 restores canonical `/var/lib/dpkg/` paths once tmpfs grows nested directories. (`242eb0a`) | **Done** |
| **dpkg query subcommands** | `dpkg -l` (list installed packages), `dpkg -s <pkg>` (raw status stanza), `dpkg -L <pkg>` (installed-file manifest) ŌĆö pure readers over the data `dpkg -i` already writes. (`9f6d859`) | **Done** |

### Wave since the M16.157 / dpkg-userland refresh

These rows land everything between commit `8faa1d0` (the docs refresh
itself) and `a73e5fb`. The headline: with the EHCI driver, userland
sockets, userland TLS and a native `apt` all in place, Hamnix can
fetch and install a Debian package over HTTPS and serve HTTP ŌĆö **all
verified under QEMU**, not on real hardware.

| Item | Description | Status |
|------|-------------|--------|
| **tmpfs V1 ŌĆö nested dirs** | `fs/tmpfs.ad` gained nested directories + a real `mkdir` body, lifting the flat-namespace / 32-byte-name-cap restriction the dpkg V1 row works around. (`dcf30f3`) | **Done** |
